         <h3><a id="user-content-tumblr-oauth-1a" class="anchor" href="#tumblr-oauth-1a" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Tumblr OAuth (1.a)</h3> 
         <p>You will first need to <a href="http://www.tumblr.com/oauth/register">register an app</a> to get the consumer key and secret. During registration of your new app, enter a "Default callback URL" of "http://:/auth/tumblr/callback". Once you register your app, copy down your "OAuth Consumer Key" and "Secret Key" and proceed below.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tumblr</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">consumerKey</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CONSUMER KEY HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">consumerSecret</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CONSUMER SECRET HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">sess</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessSecret</span>, <span class="pl-smi">user</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span></span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> e.g.,</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> return usersByTumblrName[user.name] || (usersByTumblrName[user.name] = user);</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure more parameters (most are set to defaults) via the same chainable API:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tumblr</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/tumblr<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/tumblr/callback<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you want to see what the current value of a configured parameter is, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tumblr</span>.<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/tumblr/callback'</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tumblr</span>.<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/tumblr'</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>To see all parameters that are configurable, the following will return an object whose parameter name keys map to description values:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">tumblr</span>.<span class="pl-en">configurable</span>();</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-evernote-oauth-1a" class="anchor" href="#evernote-oauth-1a" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Evernote OAuth (1.a)</h3> 
         <p>You will first need to <a href="http://www.evernote.com/about/developer/api/#key">request an API key</a> to get the consumer key and secret. Note that this consumer key and secret will only be valid for the sandbox rather than the production OAuth host. By default the Evernote module will use the production host, so you'll need to override this using the chainable API if you're using the sandbox.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">evernote</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">consumerKey</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CONSUMER KEY HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">consumerSecret</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CONSUMER SECRET HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">sess</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessSecret</span>, <span class="pl-smi">user</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span></span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> e.g.,</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> return usersByEvernoteId[user.userId] || (usersByEvernoteId[user.userId] = user);</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure more parameters (most are set to defaults) via the same chainable API:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">evernote</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">oauthHost</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://sandbox.evernote.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/evernote<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/evernote/callback<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you want to see what the current value of a configured parameter is, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">evernote</span>.<span class="pl-en">oauthHost</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 'https://sandbox.evernote.com'</span>

           </svg></a>OpenStreetMap OAuth</h3> 
         <p>You will first need to <a href="http://www.openstreetmap.org">login to OpenStreetMap</a>. Then register you application on your OpenStreetMap user page via the View my OAuth details link on the bottom of the page to get the consumer key and secret. The registered application does not need any permission listed there to login via OAuth.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span></span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> e.g.,</span>

  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-soundcloud-oauth2" class="anchor" href="#soundcloud-oauth2" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>SoundCloud OAuth2</h3> 
         <p>You will first need to <a href="http://soundcloud.com/you/apps">register an app</a> to get the client id and secret. During registration of your new app, enter a "Default callback URL" of "http://:/auth/soundcloud/callback". Once you register your app, copy down your "Client ID" and "Client Secret" and proceed below.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">soundcloud</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">appId</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CLIENT ID HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">appSecret</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CLIENT SECRET HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">handleAuthCallbackError</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">req</span>, <span class="pl-smi">res</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> TODO - Update this documentation</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> This configurable route handler defines how you want to respond to</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> a response from SoundCloud that something went wrong during the oauth2 process.</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> If you do not configure this, everyauth renders a default fallback</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> view notifying the user that their authentication failed and why.</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessTokenExtra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">soundcloudUserMetadata</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Return a user or Promise that promises a user</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Promises are created via</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>     var promise = this.Promise();</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure more parameters (most are set to defaults) via the same chainable API:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">soundcloud</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/soundcloud<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/soundcloud/callback<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you want to see what the current value of a configured parameter is, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">soundcloud</span>.<span class="pl-c1">scope</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> undefined</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">soundcloud</span>.<span class="pl-c1">display</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> undefined</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">soundcloud</span>.<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/soundcloud'</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>To see all parameters that are configurable, the following will return an object whose parameter name keys map to description values:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">soundcloud</span>.<span class="pl-en">configurable</span>();</pre>
         </div>

         <h3><a id="user-content-mailchimp-oauth2" class="anchor" href="#mailchimp-oauth2" aria-hidden="true">

  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()

  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()

         <h3><a id="user-content-mendeley-oauth-10" class="anchor" href="#mendeley-oauth-10" aria-hidden="true">

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> e.g.,</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> return usersByMendeleyId[user.main.profile_id] || (usersByMendeleyId[user.main.profile_id] = user);</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()

         <h3><a id="user-content-openid-protocol" class="anchor" href="#openid-protocol" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>OpenID protocol</h3> 
         <p>OpenID protocol allows you to use an openid auth request. You can read more information about it here <a href="http://openid.net/">http://openid.net/</a></p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">openid</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">myHostname</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>http://localhost:3000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">simpleRegistration</span>({
      <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>nickname<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>email<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>    <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>fullname<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>dob<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>      <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>gender<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>   <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>postcode<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>country<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>  <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>language<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>timezone<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
  })
	.<span class="pl-en">attributeExchange</span>({
      <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/contact/email<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>       <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/namePerson/friendly<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/namePerson<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>          <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/namePerson/first<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>    <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/contact/country/home<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/media/image/default<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
    , <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://axschema.org/x/media/signature<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>   <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>required<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">openidURLField</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>openid_identifier<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>The POST variable used to get the OpenID</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">openIdUserAttributes</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-google-openidoauth-hybrid-protocol" class="anchor" href="#google-openidoauth-hybrid-protocol" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Google OpenID+OAuth Hybrid protocol</h3> 
         <p>OpenID+OAuth Hybrid protocol allows you to combine an openid auth request with a oauth access request. You can read more information about it here <a href="http://code.google.com/apis/accounts/docs/OpenID.html">http://code.google.com/apis/accounts/docs/OpenID.html</a></p> 
         <p>Register your domain with Google <a href="https://accounts.google.com/ManageDomains">here</a> and write down the consumer key and consumer secret generated during the domain registration.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">googlehybrid</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">consumerKey</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CONSUMER KEY HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">consumerSecret</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CONSUMER SECRET HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-c1">scope</span>([<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>GOOGLE API SCOPE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>GOOGLE API SCOPE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>])
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span>(<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">userAttributes</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-boxnet" class="anchor" href="#boxnet" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Box.net</h3> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">apiKey</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR API KEY<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">sess</span>, <span class="pl-smi">authToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">boxUser</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span></span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> e.g.,</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> return usersByBoxId[user.user_id] || (usersByBoxId[user.user_id] = user);</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure more parameters (most are set to defaults) via the same chainable API:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/box<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/box/callback<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you want to see what the current value of a configured parameter is, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>.<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/box/callback'</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>.<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/box'</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>To see all parameters that are configurable, the following will return an object whose parameter name keys map to description values:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>.<span class="pl-en">configurable</span>();</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-ldap" class="anchor" href="#ldap" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>LDAP</h3> 
         <p>The LDAP module is not tested throughly yet, however it is used in production by some organizations already. Feedback is very welcome.</p> 
         <p>Install OpenLDAP client libraries:</p> 
         <pre><code>$ sudo apt-get install ldap-utils
</code></pre> 
         <p>Install <a href="https://github.com/marek-obuchowicz/node-ldapauth">node-ldapauth</a>:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">ldap</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">ldapUrl</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>ldap(s)://your.ldap.host<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">adminDn</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>DN for bind<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">adminPassword</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Password for bind user<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">searchBase</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e.g. ou=users,dc=example,dc=com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">searchFilter</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e.g. (uid={{username}})<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">requireGroupDn</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>e.g. cn=Administrators,ou=Groups,dc=example,dc=com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> The `ldap` module inherits from the `password` module, so </span>
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> refer to the `password` module instructions several sections above</span>
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> in this README.</span>
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> You do not need to configure the `authenticate` step as instructed</span>
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> by `password` because the `ldap` module already does that for you.</span>
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Moreover, all the registration related steps and configurable parameters</span>
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> are no longer valid</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">getLoginPath</span>(<span class="pl-k">...</span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">postLoginPath</span>(<span class="pl-k">...</span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">loginView</span>(<span class="pl-k">...</span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">loginSuccessRedirect</span>(<span class="pl-k">...</span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-windows-azure-access-control-service-acs" class="anchor" href="#windows-azure-access-control-service-acs" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Windows Azure Access Control Service (ACS)</h3> 
         <p>You will need to create a <a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windowsazure/hh674478.aspx">Windows Azure ACS namespace</a>. The only caveat when creating the namespace is setting the "Return URL". You will probably <a href="http://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/windowsazure/gg429779.aspx">create one Relying Party</a> for each environment (dev, qa, prod) and each of them will have a different "Return URL". For instance, dev will be <code>http://localhost:port/auth/azureacs/callback</code> and prod could be <code>https://myapp.com/auth/azureacs/callback</code> (notice the <code>/auth/azureacs/callback</code>, that's where the module will listen the POST with the token from ACS)</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">azureacs</span>
      .<span class="pl-en">identityProviderUrl</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://YOURNAMESPACE.accesscontrol.windows.net/v2/wsfederation/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
      .<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/azureacs<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
      .<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/azureacs/callback<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
      .<span class="pl-en">signingKey</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>d0jul....YOUR_SIGNINGK=_KEY......OEvz24=<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
      .<span class="pl-en">realm</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR_APPLICATION_REALM_IDENTIFIER<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
      .<span class="pl-en">homeRealm</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span><span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> if you want to use a default idp (like google/liveid)</span>
      .<span class="pl-en">tokenFormat</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>swt<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> only swt supported for now</span>
      .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">acsUser</span>) {
         <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> you could enrich the "user" entity by storing/fetching the user from a db</span>
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;
      });
      .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);


<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you want to see what the current value of a configured parameter is, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>.<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/azureacs/callback'</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>To see all parameters that are configurable, the following will return an object whose parameter name keys map to description values:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">box</span>.<span class="pl-en">configurable</span>();</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-shopify" class="anchor" href="#shopify" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Shopify</h3> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>../index<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>require('everyauth')</span>
  , express <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>express<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

everyauth
  .<span class="pl-smi">shopify</span>
    .<span class="pl-en">apiHost</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://SHOPNAME.myshopify.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) 
    .<span class="pl-en">oauthHost</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://SHOPNAME.myshopify.com<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) 
    .<span class="pl-en">appId</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR APP API KEY<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
    .<span class="pl-en">appSecret</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR APP SHARED SECRET<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>Shopify requires scope, even if you only want to use default scope</span>
    .<span class="pl-c1">scope</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>read_products,write_themes<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) 
    .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">sess</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessSecret</span>, <span class="pl-smi">shopifyUser</span>) {
      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
    })
    .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> app <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">express</span>();

<span class="pl-smi">app</span>.<span class="pl-en">use</span>(<span class="pl-smi">express</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>())
  .<span class="pl-en">use</span>(<span class="pl-smi">express</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>))
  .<span class="pl-en">use</span>(<span class="pl-smi">express</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>())
  .<span class="pl-en">use</span>(<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>(app));

<span class="pl-smi">app</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">req</span>, <span class="pl-smi">res</span>) {

});

<span class="pl-smi">app</span>.<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-stripe" class="anchor" href="#stripe" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Stripe</h3> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> everyauth <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>everyauth<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  , connect <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">require</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>connect<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">stripe</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">appId</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CLIENT ID HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">appSecret</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>YOUR CLIENT SECRET HERE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-c1">scope</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>read_only<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Defaults to read_only - can be set to 'read_write'.  See https://stripe.com/docs/connect/reference</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">landing</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>login<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>Defaults to login - can be set to 'register'.  See https://stripe.com/docs/connect/reference</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">handleAuthCallbackError</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">req</span>, <span class="pl-smi">res</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> If a user denies your app, Stripe will redirect the user to</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> /auth/facebook/callback?error=access_denied</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> This configurable route handler defines how you want to respond to</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> that.</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> If you do not configure this, everyauth renders a default fallback</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> view notifying the user that their authentication failed and why.</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessTokenExtra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">stripeUserMetadata</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Return a user or Promise that promises a user</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Promises are created via</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>     var promise = this.Promise();</span>
  })
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-en">routes</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">app</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Define your routes here</span>
};

<span class="pl-en">connect</span>(
    <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">bodyParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">cookieParser</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">session</span>({secret<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>whodunnit<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>})
  , <span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-en">middleware</span>()
  , <span class="pl-smi">connect</span>.<span class="pl-en">router</span>(routes);
).<span class="pl-en">listen</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure more parameters (most are set to defaults) via the same chainable API:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">stripe</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/stripe<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/stripe/callback<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>)
  .<span class="pl-en">redirectPath</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/auth/stripe<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>If you want to see what the current value of a configured parameter is, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">stripe</span>.<span class="pl-c1">scope</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> undefined</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">stripe</span>.<span class="pl-en">entryPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> '/auth/stripe'</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>To see all parameters that are configurable, the following will return an object whose parameter name keys map to description values:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">stripe</span>.<span class="pl-en">configurable</span>();</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-salesforce" class="anchor" href="#salesforce" aria-hidden="true">

            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Salesforce</h3> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">

  .<span class="pl-c1">scope</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>api refresh_token<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>) <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Is none are set, it defaults to 'id api refresh_token') - see http://wiki.developerforce.com/page/Digging_Deeper_into_OAuth_2.0_on_Force.com</span>

         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-configuring-a-module" class="anchor" href="#configuring-a-module" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Configuring a Module</h2> 
         <p>everyauth was built with powerful configuration needs in mind.</p> 
         <p>Every module comes with a set of parameters that you can configure directly. To see a list of those parameters on a per module basis, with descriptions about what they do, enter the following into the node REPL (to access the REPL, just type <code>node</code> at the command line)</p> 
         <pre><code>&gt; var ea = require('everyauth');
&gt; ea.facebook.configurable();
</code></pre> 
         <p>For example, you will see that one of the configuration parameters is <code>moduleTimeout</code>, which is described to be <code>how long to wait per step before timing out and invoking any timeout callbacks</code></p> 
         <p>Every configuration parameter corresponds to a method of the same name on the auth module under consideration (i.e., in this case <code>ea.facebook</code>). To create or over-write that parameter, just call that method with the new value as the argument:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">ea</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">moduleTimeout</span>( <span class="pl-c1">4000</span> ); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Wait 4 seconds before timing out any step</span>
                          <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> involved in the facebook auth process</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Configuration parameters can be scalars. But they can be anything. For example, they can also be functions, too. The facebook module has a configurable step named <code>findOrCreateUser</code> that is described as "STEP FN [findOrCreateUser] function encapsulating the logic for the step <code>fetchOAuthUser</code>.". What this means is that this configures the function (i.e., "FN") that encapsulates the logic of this step.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">ea</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">extra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oauthUser</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> find or create user logic goes here</span>
  });</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>How do we know what arguments the function takes? We elaborate more about step function configuration in our <code>Introspection</code> section below.</p> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-for-coffee-script-lovers" class="anchor" href="#for-coffee-script-lovers" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>For coffee-script lovers</h3> 
         <p>Everyauth also supports a special method <code>configure</code> for coffee-script aficionados. Coffee and chainable APIs often don't mix well. As an alternative, you can configure an everyauth module using an <code>Object</code> passed to <code>configure</code>:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-coffee">
          <pre>everyauth.dropbox.configure
  <span class="pl-v">consumerKey</span>:       conf.dropbox.consumerKey
  <span class="pl-v">consumerSecret</span>:    conf.dropbox.consumerSecret
  <span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span><span class="pl-k">:</span><span class="pl-smi">  <span class="pl-smi">(sess, accessToken, accessSecret, dbMeta)</span></span> <span class="pl-k"><span class="pl-k">-&gt;</span></span> users[dbMeta.uid] <span class="pl-k">or=</span> <span class="pl-en">addUser</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>dropbox<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, dbMeta)
  <span class="pl-v">redirectPath</span>:      <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-introspection" class="anchor" href="#introspection" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Introspection</h2> 
         <p>everyauth provides convenient methods and getters for finding out about any module.</p> 
         <p>Show all configurable parameters with their descriptions:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-en">configurable</span>();</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Show the value of a single configurable parameter:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Get the value of the configurable callbackPath parameter</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-en">callbackPath</span>(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> =&gt; '/auth/facebook/callback'</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Show the declared routes (pretty printed):</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-smi">routes</span>;</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Show the steps initiated by a given route:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-smi">route</span>.<span class="pl-smi">get</span>.<span class="pl-smi">entryPath</span>.<span class="pl-smi">steps</span>; 
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-smi">route</span>.<span class="pl-smi">get</span>.<span class="pl-smi">callbackPath</span>.<span class="pl-smi">steps</span>;</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Sometimes you need to set up additional steps for a given auth module, by defining that step in your app. For example, the set of steps triggered when someone requests the facebook module's <code>callbackPath</code> contains a step that you must define in your app. To see what that step is, you can introspect the <code>callbackPath</code> route with the facebook module.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-smi">route</span>.<span class="pl-smi">get</span>.<span class="pl-smi">callbackPath</span>.<span class="pl-smi">steps</span>.<span class="pl-smi">incomplete</span>;
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> =&gt; [ { name: 'findOrCreateUser',</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>        error: 'is missing: its function' } ]</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>This tells you that you must define the function that defines the logic for the <code>findOrCreateUser</code> step. To see what the function signature looks like for this step:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> matchingStep <span class="pl-k">=</span>
<span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-smi">route</span>.<span class="pl-smi">get</span>.<span class="pl-smi">callbackPath</span>.<span class="pl-smi">steps</span>.<span class="pl-en">filter</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">step</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">step</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span> <span class="pl-k">===</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>findOrCreateUser<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;
})[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>];
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> { name: 'findOrCreateUser',</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>   accepts: [ 'session', 'accessToken', 'extra', 'oauthUser' ],</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>   promises: [ 'user' ] }</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>This tells you that the function should take the following 4 arguments:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">extra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oauthUser</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">...</span>
}</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>And that the function should return a <code>user</code> that is a user object or a Promise that promises a user object.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> For synchronous lookup situations, you can return a user</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">extra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oauthUser</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">...</span>
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> { id<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>some user id<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, username<span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>some user name<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> };
}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> OR</span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> For asynchronous lookup situations, you must return a Promise that</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> will be fulfilled with a user later on</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">extra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oauthUser</span>) {
  <span class="pl-k">var</span> promise <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">this</span>.<span class="pl-en">Promise</span>();
  <span class="pl-en">asyncFindUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">err</span>, <span class="pl-smi">user</span>) {
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> (err) <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-smi">promise</span>.<span class="pl-en">fail</span>(err);
    <span class="pl-smi">promise</span>.<span class="pl-en">fulfill</span>(user);
  });
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> promise;
}</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You add this function as the block for the step <code>findOrCreateUser</code> just like you configure any other configurable parameter in your auth module:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>
  .<span class="pl-en">findOrCreateUser</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">session</span>, <span class="pl-smi">accessToken</span>, <span class="pl-smi">extra</span>, <span class="pl-smi">oauthUser</span>) {
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Logic goes here</span>
  });</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>There are also several other introspection tools at your disposal:</p> 
         <p>For example, to show the submodules of an auth module by name:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">oauth2</span>.<span class="pl-smi">submodules</span>;</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Other introspection tools to describe (explanations coming soon):</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li> <p><em>Invalid Steps</em></p> 
           <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
            <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-smi">routes</span>.<span class="pl-smi">get</span>.<span class="pl-smi">callbackPath</span>.<span class="pl-smi">steps</span>.<span class="pl-smi">invalid</span></pre>
           </div> </li> 
         </ul> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-debugging" class="anchor" href="#debugging" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Debugging</h2> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-debugging---logging-module-steps" class="anchor" href="#debugging---logging-module-steps" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Debugging - Logging Module Steps</h3> 
         <p>To turn on debugging:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">debug</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>Each everyauth auth strategy module is composed of steps. As each step begins and ends, everyauth will print out to the console the beginning and end of each step. So by turning on the debug flag, you get insight into what step everyauth is executing at any time.</p> 
         <p>For example, here is some example debugging information output to the console during a Facebook Connect authorization:</p> 
         <pre><code>starting step - getAuthUri
...finished step
starting step - requestAuthUri
...finished step
starting step - getCode
...finished step
starting step - getAccessToken
...finished step
starting step - fetchOAuthUser
...finished step
starting step - getSession
...finished step
starting step - findOrCreateUser
...finished step
starting step - compile
...finished step
starting step - addToSession
...finished step
starting step - sendResponse
...finished step
</code></pre> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-debugging---configuring-error-handling" class="anchor" href="#debugging---configuring-error-handling" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Debugging - Configuring Error Handling</h3> 
         <p>By default, all modules handle errors by throwing them. That said, <code>everyauth</code> allows you to over-ride this behavior.</p> 
         <p>You can configure error handling at the module and step level. To handle <em>all</em> errors in the same manner across all auth modules that you use, do the following.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">everymodule</span>.<span class="pl-en">moduleErrback</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Do something with the err -- e.g., log it, throw it</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure your error handling on a per module basis. So, for example, if you want to handle errors during the Facebook module differently than in other modules:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-en">moduleErrback</span>( <span class="pl-k">function</span> (<span class="pl-smi">err</span>) {
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Do something with the err -- e.g., log it, throw it</span>
});</pre>
         </div> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-debugging---setting-timeouts" class="anchor" href="#debugging---setting-timeouts" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>Debugging - Setting Timeouts</h3> 
         <p>By default, every module has 10 seconds to complete each step. If a step takes longer than 10 seconds to complete, then everyauth will pass a timeout error to your configured error handler (see section "Configure Error Handling" above).</p> 
         <p>If you would like to increase or decrease the timeout period across all modules, you can do so via:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">everymodule</span>.<span class="pl-en">moduleTimeout</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2000</span>); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Wait 2 seconds per step instead before timing out</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can eliminate the timeout altogether by configuring your timeouts to -1:</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">everymodule</span>.<span class="pl-en">moduleTimeout</span>(<span class="pl-k">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>);</pre>
         </div> 
         <p>You can also configure the timeout period on a per module basis. For example, the following will result in the facebook module having 3 seconds to complete each step before timing out; all other modules will have the default 10 seconds per step before timing out.</p> 
         <div class="highlight highlight-source-js">
          <pre><span class="pl-smi">everyauth</span>.<span class="pl-smi">facebook</span>.<span class="pl-en">moduleTimeout</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3000</span>); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> Wait 3 seconds</span></pre>
         </div> 
         <h2><a id="user-content-in-the-wild" class="anchor" href="#in-the-wild" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
           </svg></a>In the Wild</h2> 
         <p>The following projects use everyauth.</p> 
         <p>If you are using everyauth in a project, app, or module, get on the list below by getting in touch or submitting a pull request with changes to the README.</p> 
         <h3><a id="user-content-startups--apps" class="anchor" href="#startups--apps" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>

            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>

         <h2><a id="user-content-tutorials" class="anchor" href="#tutorials" aria-hidden="true">

            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>

         <h2><a id="user-content-author" class="anchor" href="#author" aria-hidden="true">
           <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
